On Friday, the Commerce Department released 1,320 pages of internal memos, emails and other documents related to Ross's decision as part of the lawsuits against the citizenship question.
Ross said the driving force behind the question is the need for more accurate citizenship data. Critics of the question ‚Äî more than two dozen states and cities ‚Äî are skeptical. They are concerned that the question will discourage noncitizens from participating.
Emails and memos show Commerce Secretary Wilbur Ross overruled Census Bureau concerns and was urged to exclude noncitizens from census numbers used to reallocate congressional seats. https://t.co/c4etLxT4FO
